omur yavuz <omur.yavuz@...>
2012-04-05 15:14:30 GMT

hi ,

I'm trying to compile udig product  following sdk quickstart. but after run udig cannot load project explorer and layers window. At dependencies tab  udig-feature(1.3.qualifier) and udig_language-feature(1.3.qualifier)  missing. 

I got same error with custom application tutorial .  it looks like a tree view issue .

udig error and custom application logs are below.

My Platform :

OS : Windows 7 x64 
eclipse : 3.7.0 ( also tried with 3.7.2 too)
SDK : udig SDK 1.3.1 
Drools : 3.7.0
JRE : jre_1.6.24_ECW

Frank Gasdorf | 5 Apr 2012 20:12


Re: udig SDK 1.3.1 cannot create ProjectExplorer and Layers window

Frank Gasdorf <fgdrf@...>
2012-04-05 18:12:33 GMT
Could you please check the run configuration. To do so, please open
menu -> Run -> Run configuration

choose the one you have started before, switch to the Plug-Ins Tab and
hit the 'validate plug-ins' button to verify that everything looks
fine. If a dialog pops up and shows missing dependencies leave it and
hit "add required plug-ins"

Check again afterwards, if there is still a problem, please report
which dependencies are not resolvable.

Good luck

Frank

PS: Try to synch again in the custom product Editor (Overview tab ->
Testing section (lower left) -> Synchronize)

On Apr 5, 2012, at 9:12 PM, Frank Gasdorf wrote:

> Could you please check the run configuration. To do so, please open
> menu -> Run -> Run configuration
> 
> choose the one you have started before, switch to the Plug-Ins Tab and
> hit the 'validate plug-ins' button to verify that everything looks
> fine. If a dialog pops up and shows missing dependencies leave it and
> hit "add required plug-ins"
> 
> Check again afterwards, if there is still a problem, please report
> which dependencies are not resolvable.
> 
> Good luck
> 
> Frank
> 
> PS: Try to synch again in the custom product Editor (Overview tab ->
> Testing section (lower left) -> Synchronize)

> Could you please check the run configuration. To do so, please open
> menu -> Run -> Run configuration
> 
> choose the one you have started before, switch to the Plug-Ins Tab and
> hit the 'validate plug-ins' button to verify that everything looks
> fine. If a dialog pops up and shows missing dependencies leave it and
> hit "add required plug-ins"

> which dependencies are not resolvable.
> 
> Good luck

Re: udig SDK 1.3.1 cannot create ProjectExplorer and Layers window

Frank Gasdorf <fgdrf@...>
2012-04-05 19:30:46 GMT
Hmm, seems to me, that you need to set your target platform correctly
or import the required features (marked as missing) and dependent udig
bundles from the sdk installation folder.

Have you walked through the following documents :
* http://udig.refractions.net/confluence/display/DEV/1+SDK+Quickstart
* http://udig.refractions.net/confluence/display/DEV/3+Custom+Application+Tutorial

Have you installed Eclipse EMF or a simple Eclipse IDE for Java EE
Developers/RCP Developers?

Cheers
Frank
